 ise 1968 main rashtriya udyaan ghoshit kiya gaya tha

 Before the National Park was created, the forest around Bandhavgarh was maintained as a hunting ground for the Maharajas and their guests
 yaheen kii ek baghin sita ke naam sabase zyada baar photo khinchi jane vaali badhin kaa ricard bhi he

 har bhashaa kii tarah angreji bhashaa main achche lekhan ke liye kai sharte hai, jinhen puraa karke hi aap apane lekhan-kaushal ko dikhaa sakate hai
 1
 Time And Tense:kisi bhi copy ko likhte hue yah dhyaan dena chahie ki vaakya banaate samay aap samay or kaal ke saath ched-chhaad to nahin kar rahe hai
 Always use the same tense while saying the same thing
 example:i went to my friend's college yesterday and we played tennis together (correct)i went to my friend's college yesterday and we play tennis together (incorrect)2
 Subject Verb Agreement: Subject Verb Agreement has the biggest role in writing any sentence correctly in English
 agar aap iske niyamon ke hisaab se vaakya ko frem nahin karenge to aap kabhi bhi sahi nahin likh paaenge
 Example: Everyone has done his / her homework (correct) Everyone has done his / her homework (incorrect) 3
 Articles kaa upyog:isaki acchhee jaankaree na hone par bhale hi aap sochate hon ki iskaa prabhaav vaakya vinyas par zyada nahin padataa lekin aisa sochnagaltahai
 Articles are not used much in Hindi, but you can never write good English without knowing the article
 example:i watched a movie Yesterday (correct)i watched movie Yesterday (incorrect)4
 Correct practice of preposition: It is necessary to have basic knowledge of its rules, but the command can be found only when you remember the prepostion associated with the frail verb and words
 lagaataar likhane or practice karne se isaki acchhee jaankaree hasil kii ja sakati he
 It is necessary to read novels, newspapers and magazines to remember the prepostion
 example:i am at Work (correct)i am in Work (incorrect)5
 Always write short sentences: Whenever we write something, its purpose is to convey its point to the front
 chote vaakya bananaa aapke liye bhi aasaan hoga or padhane vaale ke liye bhi
 6
 likhte samay asamanjas main na rahen:grammer ke niyam ke mutabik agar aapako lag rahaa he ki koi vaakya sahi nahin he to use hataa hi den
 Do not think that it is right or wrong
 galat likhane se behatar he ki aap kitaab palaten or grammer ke niyam dekh len
 7
 jis bhashaa main likhen usamen hi sochen:jinaki maatrubhaashongrejinhin he, unke saath yah samasya aati he ki ve likh to angreji main hote hai lekin sochate apni maatrubhaasha main hai
 By doing this, the framing of the sentence is not good and the writer is not even aware of it
 angreji likhte vakt hameshaa angreji main hi sochen
 8
 verde aandar majboot karen:hameshaa yah koshish karen ki ek shabd duusare se judaa hua ho
 Do not leave it to others to understand what you have written
 To make it strong, you will have to know more and more words along with basic knowledge of grammar rules
